    46^I[37m;;; Commentary:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    47^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    48^I[37m;;; This file is the first thing loaded into Guile.  It adds many mundane[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    49^I[37m;;; definitions and a few that are interesting.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    50^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    51^I[37m;;; The module system (hence the hierarchical namespace) are defined in this[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    52^I[37m;;; file.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    53^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    54^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    55^I[37m;;; Code:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    56^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    57^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    58^I[37m;;; {Deprecation}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    59^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    60^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    61^I[37m;; We don't have macros here, but we do want to define[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    62^I[37m;; `begin-deprecated' early.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    63^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    64^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mbegin-deprecated[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    65^I[37m  [39;49;00m([32mprocedure->memoizing-macro[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    66^I[37m   [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mexp[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31menv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    67^I[37m     [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36minclude-deprecated-features[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    68^I[37m^I [39;49;00m`([34mbegin[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m,@([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mexp[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
    69^I[37m^I [39;49;00m`[31m#f[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
    70^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    71^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    72^I[37m;;; {Features}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    73^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    74^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    75^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mprovide[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msym[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    76^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmemq[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msym[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m*features*[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
    77^I[37m      [39;49;00m([34mset![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m*features*[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcons[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msym[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m*features*[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
    78^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    79^I[37m;;; Return #t iff FEATURE is available to this Guile interpreter.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    80^I[37m;;; In SLIB, provided? also checks to see if the module is available.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    81^I[37m;;; We should do that too, but don't.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    82^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mprovided?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfeature[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    83^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmemq[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfeature[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m*features*[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31m#t[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
    84^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    85^I([34mbegin-deprecated[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    86^I[37m [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mfeature?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msym[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    87^I[37m   [39;49;00m([36missue-deprecation-warning[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    88^I[37m    [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`feature?' is deprecated.  Use `provided?' instead.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    89^I[37m   [39;49;00m([36mprovided?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msym[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
    90^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    91^I[37m;;; let format alias simple-format until the more complete version is loaded[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    92^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mformat[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36msimple-format[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    93^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    94^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    95^I[37m;;; {R4RS compliance}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
    96^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    97^I([36mprimitive-load-path[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mice-9/r4rs.scm[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
    98^I[37m[39;49;00m$
    99^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   100^I[37m;;; {Simple Debugging Tools}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   101^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   102^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   103^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   104^I[37m;; peek takes any number of arguments, writes them to the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   105^I[37m;; current ouput port, and returns the last argument.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   106^I[37m;; It is handy to wrap around an expression to look at[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   107^I[37m;; a value each time is evaluated, e.g.:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   108^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   109^I[37m;;^I(+ 10 (troublesome-fn))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   110^I[37m;;^I=> (+ 10 (pk 'troublesome-fn-returned (troublesome-fn)))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   111^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   112^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   113^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mpeek[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   114^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mnewline[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   115^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m;;; [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   116^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mwrite[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   117^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mnewline[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   118^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlast-pair[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   119^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   120^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mpk[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mpeek[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   121^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   122^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mwarn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   123^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mwith-output-to-port[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcurrent-error-port[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   124^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m()[37m[39;49;00m$
   125^I[37m      [39;49;00m([36mnewline[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   126^I[37m      [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m;;; WARNING [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   127^I[37m      [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   128^I[37m      [39;49;00m([36mnewline[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   129^I[37m      [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlast-pair[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mstuff[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   130^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   131^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   132^I[37m;;; {Trivial Functions}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   133^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   134^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   135^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36midentity[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mx[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mx[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   136^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m1+[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36m+[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m1[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   137^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m1-[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36m+[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m-1[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   138^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mand=>[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mprocedure[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mprocedure[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   139^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-hash-table[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mk[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-vector[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mk[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m'()))[37m[39;49;00m$
   140^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   141^I([34mbegin-deprecated[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   142^I[37m [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mx[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   143^I[37m   [39;49;00m([36missue-deprecation-warning[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`id' is deprecated.  Use `identity' instead.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   144^I[37m   [39;49;00m([36midentity[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mx[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   145^I[37m [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32m-1+[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   146^I[37m   [39;49;00m([36missue-deprecation-warning[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`-1+' is deprecated.  Use `1-' instead.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   147^I[37m   [39;49;00m([36m1-[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mn[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   148^I[37m [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mreturn-it[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   149^I[37m   [39;49;00m([36missue-deprecation-warning[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m`return-it' is deprecated.  Use `noop' instead.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   150^I[37m   [39;49;00m([36mapply[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mnoop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   151^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   152^I[37m;;; apply-to-args is functionally redundant with apply and, worse,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   153^I[37m;;; is less general than apply since it only takes two arguments.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   154^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   155^I[37m;;; On the other hand, apply-to-args is a syntacticly convenient way to[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   156^I[37m;;; perform binding in many circumstances when the "let" family of[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   157^I[37m;;; of forms don't cut it.  E.g.:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   158^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   159^I[37m;;;^I(apply-to-args (return-3d-mouse-coords)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   160^I[37m;;;^I  (lambda (x y z)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   161^I[37m;;;^I^I...))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   162^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   163^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   164^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mapply-to-args[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfn[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mapply[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   165^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   166^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   167^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   168^I[37m;;; {Integer Math}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   169^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   170^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   171^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mipow-by-squaring[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mx[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mk[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31macc[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

   282^I[37m      [39;49;00m[31mnew-port[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$

   419^I[37m;;; {and-map and or-map}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   420^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   421^I[37m;;; (and-map fn lst) is like (and (fn (car lst)) (fn (cadr lst)) (fn...) ...)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   422^I[37m;;; (or-map fn lst) is like (or (fn (car lst)) (fn (cadr lst)) (fn...) ...)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   423^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   424^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   425^I[37m;; and-map f l[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   426^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   427^I[37m;; Apply f to successive elements of l until exhaustion or f returns #f.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   428^I[37m;; If returning early, return #f.  Otherwise, return the last value returned[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   429^I[37m;; by f.  If f has never been called because l is empty, return #t.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   430^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   431^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mand-map[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mf[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mlst[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

   433^I[37m^I     [39;49;00m([32ml[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mlst[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   434^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mresult[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   435^I[37m^I [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnull?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31ml[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

   437^I[37m^I     [39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mf[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31ml[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31ml[39;49;00m))))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   438^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   439^I[37m;; or-map f l[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   440^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   441^I[37m;; Apply f to successive elements of l until exhaustion or while f returns #f.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   442^I[37m;; If returning early, return the return value of f.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   443^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   444^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mor-map[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mf[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mlst[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

   646^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   647^I[37m;;; {Help for scm_shell}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   648^I[37m;;; The argument-processing code used by Guile-based shells generates[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   649^I[37m;;; Scheme code based on the argument list.  This page contains help[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   650^I[37m;;; functions for the code it generates.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   651^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   652^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcommand-line[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mprogram-arguments[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   653^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   654^I[37m;; This is mostly for the internal use of the code generated by[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   655^I[37m;; scm_compile_shell_switches.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   656^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mload-user-init[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   657^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet*[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mhome[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mgetenv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mHOME[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   658^I[37m^I^I   [39;49;00m([34mfalse-if-exception[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mpasswd:dir[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mgetpwuid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mgetuid[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   659^I[37m^I^I   [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m/[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m))[37m  [39;49;00m[37m;; fallback for cygwin etc.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   660^I[37m^I [39;49;00m([32minit-file[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36min-vicinity[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mhome[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m.guile[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   661^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mfile-exists?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minit-file[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   662^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([36mprimitive-load[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minit-file[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   663^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   664^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   665^I[37m;;; {Loading by paths}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   666^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   667^I[37m;;; Load a Scheme source file named NAME, searching for it in the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   668^I[37m;;; directories listed in %load-path, and applying each of the file[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   669^I[37m;;; name extensions listed in %load-extensions.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   670^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mload-from-path[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   671^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mstart-stack[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'load-stack[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   672^I[37m^I       [39;49;00m([36mprimitive-load-path[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   673^I[37m[39;49;00m$

   906^I[37m^I^I^I^I^I^I   [39;49;00m([34melse[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopts[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   907^I[37m^I^I^I^I^I    [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mcase[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   908^I[37m^I^I^I^I    [39;49;00m[31mcases[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   909^I[37m    [39;49;00m`([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32m%display-usage[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m()[37m [39;49;00m([32mdisplay-usage-report[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m',usage-desc[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   910^I[37m       [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32m%argv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   911^I[37m^I [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%next-arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32m%argv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%argv[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   912^I[37m^I   [39;49;00m([32mget-option[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%argv[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   913^I[37m^I^I       [39;49;00m[33m',kw-opts[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   914^I[37m^I^I       [39;49;00m[33m',kw-args[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   915^I[37m^I^I       [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32m%opt[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%new-argv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   916^I[37m^I^I^I [39;49;00m([34mcase[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m%opt[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   917^I[37m^I^I^I   [39;49;00m,@[37m [39;49;00m[31mtransmogrified-cases[39;49;00m))))))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   918^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   919^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   920^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   921^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   922^I[37m;;; {Low Level Modules}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   923^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   924^I[37m;;; These are the low level data structures for modules.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   925^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   926^I[37m;;; !!! warning: The interface to lazy binder procedures is going[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   927^I[37m;;; to be changed in an incompatible way to permit all the basic[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   928^I[37m;;; module ops to be virtualized.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   929^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   930^I[37m;;; (make-module size use-list lazy-binding-proc) => module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   931^I[37m;;; module-{obarray,uses,binder}[|-set!][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   932^I[37m;;; (module? obj) => [#t|#f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   933^I[37m;;; (module-locally-bound? module symbol) => [#t|#f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   934^I[37m;;; (module-bound? module symbol) => [#t|#f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   935^I[37m;;; (module-symbol-locally-interned? module symbol) => [#t|#f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   936^I[37m;;; (module-symbol-interned? module symbol) => [#t|#f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   937^I[37m;;; (module-local-variable module symbol) => [#<variable ...> | #f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   938^I[37m;;; (module-variable module symbol) => [#<variable ...> | #f][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   939^I[37m;;; (module-symbol-binding module symbol opt-value)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   940^I[37m;;;^I^I=> [ <obj> | opt-value | an error occurs ][39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   941^I[37m;;; (module-make-local-var! module symbol) => #<variable...>[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   942^I[37m;;; (module-add! module symbol var) => unspecified[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   943^I[37m;;; (module-remove! module symbol) =>  unspecified[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   944^I[37m;;; (module-for-each proc module) => unspecified[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   945^I[37m;;; (make-scm-module) => module ; a lazy copy of the symhash module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   946^I[37m;;; (set-current-module module) => unspecified[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   947^I[37m;;; (current-module) => #<module...>[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   948^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   949^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   950^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   951^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   952^I[37m;;; {Printing Modules}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   953^I[37m;; This is how modules are printed.  You can re-define it.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   954^I[37m;; (Redefining is actually more complicated than simply redefining[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   955^I[37m;; %print-module because that would only change the binding and not[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   956^I[37m;; the value stored in the vtable that determines how record are[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   957^I[37m;; printed. Sigh.)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   958^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   959^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m%print-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m  [39;49;00m[37m; unused args: depth length style table)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   960^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m#<[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   961^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-kind[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mmodule[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   962^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-name[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
   963^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   964^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([34mbegin[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   965^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   966^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
   967^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   968^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnumber->string[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mobject-address[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[34m16[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   969^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mdisplay[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33m>[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mport[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   970^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   971^I[37m;; module-type[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   972^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   973^I[37m;; A module is characterized by an obarray in which local symbols[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   974^I[37m;; are interned, a list of modules, "uses", from which non-local[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   975^I[37m;; bindings can be inherited, and an optional lazy-binder which[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   976^I[37m;; is a (CLOSURE module symbol) which, as a last resort, can provide[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   977^I[37m;; bindings that would otherwise not be found locally in the module.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   978^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   979^I[37m;; NOTE: If you change here, you also need to change libguile/modules.h.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   980^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   981^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   982^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mmake-record-type[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   983^I[37m^I^I    [39;49;00m'([31mobarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31muses[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbinder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31meval-closure[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mtransformer[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkind[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   984^I[37m^I^I^I      [39;49;00m[31mobservers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mweak-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mobserver-id[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   985^I[37m^I^I    [39;49;00m[36m%print-module[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   986^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   987^I[37m;; make-module &opt size uses binder[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   988^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   989^I[37m;; Create a new module, perhaps with a particular size of obarray,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
   990^I[37m;; initial uses list, or binding procedure.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

   994^I[37m[39;49;00m$
   995^I[37m      [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mparse-arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mindex[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mdefault[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   996^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m>[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlength[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mindex[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   997^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m([36mlist-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mindex[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
   998^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m[31mdefault[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
   999^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1000^I[37m      [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m>[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlength[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[34m3[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1001^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mToo many args to make-module.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31margs[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1002^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1003^I[37m      [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32msize[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mparse-arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m0[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m1021[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1004^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m([32muses[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mparse-arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m1[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m'()))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1005^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m([32mbinder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mparse-arg[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m2[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1006^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1007^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36minteger?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msize[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1008^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mIllegal size to make-module.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msize[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1009^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mlist?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31muses[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

  1011^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mIncorrect use list.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31muses[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1012^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbinder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mprocedure?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbinder[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1013^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1014^I[37m^I     [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mLazy-binder expected to be a procedure or #f.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbinder[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1015^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1016^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-constructor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-vector[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31msize[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m'())[37m[39;49;00m$
  1017^I[37m^I^I^I^I^I  [39;49;00m[31muses[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbinder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1018^I[37m^I^I^I^I^I  [39;49;00m'()[37m[39;49;00m$
  1019^I[37m^I^I^I^I^I  [39;49;00m([36mmake-weak-value-hash-table[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m31[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1020^I[37m^I^I^I^I^I  [39;49;00m[34m0[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1021^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1022^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m[37m;; We can't pass this as an argument to module-constructor,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1023^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m[37m;; because we need it to close over a pointer to the module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1024^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m[37m;; itself.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1025^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m([32mset-module-eval-closure![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mstandard-eval-closure[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1026^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1027^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1028^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1029^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-constructor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mrecord-constructor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1030^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-obarray[39;49;00m[37m  [39;49;00m([36mrecord-accessor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'obarray[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$

  1054^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([36msetter[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mrecord-modifier[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule-type[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'eval-closure[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1055^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mclosure[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

  1057^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m;; Make it possible to lookup the module from the environment.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1058^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m;; This implementation is correct since an eval closure can belong[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1059^I[37m      [39;49;00m[37m;; to maximally one module.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1060^I[37m      [39;49;00m([36mset-procedure-property![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mclosure[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m'module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1061^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1062^I([34mbegin-deprecated[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1063^I[37m [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32meval-in-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mexp[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

  1066^I[37m   [39;49;00m([36meval[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mexp[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmod[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1067^I[37m[39;49;00m$

  1074^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mcons[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1075^I[37m[39;49;00m$

  1077^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mmodule-observer-id[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1078^I[37m    [39;49;00m([36mhash-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-weak-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

  1080^I[37m    [39;49;00m([36mcons[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1081^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1082^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-unobserve[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mtoken[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1083^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mtoken[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1084^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([32mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mtoken[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1085^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36minteger?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1086^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([36mhash-remove![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-weak-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1087^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([36mset-module-observers![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mdelq1![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1088^I[37m  [39;49;00m[34m*unspecified*[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1089^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1090^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-modified[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1091^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mfor-each[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mproc[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([32mproc[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1092^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mhash-fold[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mid[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mproc[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mres[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([32mproc[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-weak-observers[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1093^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1094^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1095^I[37m;;; {Module Searching in General}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1096^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1097^I[37m;;; We sometimes want to look for properties of a symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1098^I[37m;;; just within the obarray of one module.  If the property[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1099^I[37m;;; holds, then it is said to hold ``locally'' as in, ``The symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1100^I[37m;;; DISPLAY is locally rebound in the module `safe-guile'.''[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1101^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1102^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1103^I[37m;;; Other times, we want to test for a symbol property in the obarray[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1104^I[37m;;; of M and, if it is not found there, try each of the modules in the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1105^I[37m;;; uses list of M.  This is the normal way of testing for some[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1106^I[37m;;; property, so we state these properties without qualification as[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1107^I[37m;;; in: ``The symbol 'fnord is interned in module M because it is[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1108^I[37m;;; interned locally in module M2 which is a member of the uses list[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1109^I[37m;;; of M.''[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1110^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1111^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1112^I[37m;; module-search fn m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1113^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1114^I[37m;; return the first non-#f result of FN applied to M and then to[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1115^I[37m;; the modules in the uses of m, and so on recursively.  If all applications[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1116^I[37m;; return #f, then so does this function.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1117^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1118^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-search[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1119^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mpos[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1120^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mpair?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mpos[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1121^I[37m^I [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-search[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mfn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mpos[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1122^I[37m^I     [39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mpos[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1123^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mfn[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1124^I[37m      [39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-uses[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1125^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1126^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1127^I[37m;;; {Is a symbol bound in a module?}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1128^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1129^I[37m;;; Symbol S in Module M is bound if S is interned in M and if the binding[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1130^I[37m;;; of S in M has been set to some well-defined value.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1131^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1132^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1133^I[37m;; module-locally-bound? module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1134^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1135^I[37m;; Is a symbol bound (interned and defined) locally in a given module?[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1136^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1137^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-locally-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1138^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1139^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1140^I[37m^I [39;49;00m([36mvariable-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1141^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1142^I[37m;; module-bound? module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1143^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1144^I[37m;; Is a symbol bound (interned and defined) anywhere in a given module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1145^I[37m;; or its uses?[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1146^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1147^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1148^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-search[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-locally-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1149^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1150^I[37m;;; {Is a symbol interned in a module?}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1151^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1152^I[37m;;; Symbol S in Module M is interned if S occurs in[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1153^I[37m;;; of S in M has been set to some well-defined value.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1154^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1155^I[37m;;; It is possible to intern a symbol in a module without providing[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1156^I[37m;;; an initial binding for the corresponding variable.  This is done[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1157^I[37m;;; with:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1158^I[37m;;;       (module-add! module symbol (make-undefined-variable))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1159^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1160^I[37m;;; In that case, the symbol is interned in the module, but not[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1161^I[37m;;; bound there.  The unbound symbol shadows any binding for that[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1162^I[37m;;; symbol that might otherwise be inherited from a member of the uses list.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1163^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1164^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1165^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-get-handle[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1166^I[37m  [39;49;00m(([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36msymbol?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[36mhashq-get-handle[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mhash-get-handle[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1167^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1168^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1169^I[37m  [39;49;00m(([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36msymbol?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[36mhashq-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mhash-ref[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1170^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1171^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1172^I[37m  [39;49;00m(([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36msymbol?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[36mhashq-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mhash-set![39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1173^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1174^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-remove![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1175^I[37m  [39;49;00m(([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36msymbol?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[36mhashq-remove![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mhash-remove![39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mob[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mkey[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1176^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1177^I[37m;; module-symbol-locally-interned? module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1178^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1179^I[37m;; is a symbol interned (not neccessarily defined) locally in a given module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1180^I[37m;; or its uses?  Interned symbols shadow inherited bindings even if[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1181^I[37m;; they are not themselves bound to a defined value.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1182^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1183^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-symbol-locally-interned?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1184^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-get-handle[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1185^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1186^I[37m;; module-symbol-interned? module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1187^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1188^I[37m;; is a symbol interned (not neccessarily defined) anywhere in a given module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1189^I[37m;; or its uses?  Interned symbols shadow inherited bindings even if[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1190^I[37m;; they are not themselves bound to a defined value.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1191^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1192^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-symbol-interned?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1193^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-search[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-symbol-locally-interned?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1194^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1195^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1196^I[37m;;; {Mapping modules x symbols --> variables}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1197^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1198^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1199^I[37m;; module-local-variable module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1200^I[37m;; return the local variable associated with a MODULE and SYMBOL.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1201^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1202^I[37m;;; This function is very important. It is the only function that can[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1203^I[37m;;; return a variable from a module other than the mutators that store[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1204^I[37m;;; new variables in modules.  Therefore, this function is the location[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1205^I[37m;;; of the "lazy binder" hack.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1206^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1207^I[37m;;; If symbol is defined in MODULE, and if the definition binds symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1208^I[37m;;; to a variable, return that variable object.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1209^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1210^I[37m;;; If the symbols is not found at first, but the module has a lazy binder,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1211^I[37m;;; then try the binder.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1212^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1213^I[37m;;; If the symbol is not found at all, return #f.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1214^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1215^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1216^I[37m;  (caddr[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1217^I[37m;   (list m v[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1218^I[37m^I [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mb[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1219^I[37m^I   [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mvariable?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mb[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mb[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1220^I[37m^I       [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-binder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1221^I[37m^I^I    [39;49;00m(([36mmodule-binder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1222^I[37m;))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1223^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1224^I[37m;; module-variable module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1225^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1226^I[37m;; like module-local-variable, except search the uses in the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1227^I[37m;; case V is not found in M.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1228^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1229^I[37m;; NOTE: This function is superseded with C code (see modules.c)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1230^I[37m;;;      when using the standard eval closure.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1231^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1232^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1233^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-search[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1234^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1235^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1236^I[37m;;; {Mapping modules x symbols --> bindings}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1237^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1238^I[37m;;; These are similar to the mapping to variables, except that the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1239^I[37m;;; variable is dereferenced.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1240^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1241^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1242^I[37m;; module-symbol-binding module symbol opt-value[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1243^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1244^I[37m;; return the binding of a variable specified by name within[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1245^I[37m;; a given module, signalling an error if the variable is unbound.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1246^I[37m;; If the OPT-VALUE is passed, then instead of signalling an error,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1247^I[37m;; return OPT-VALUE.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1248^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1249^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-symbol-local-binding[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1250^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1251^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1252^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([36mvariable-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1253^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnull?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1254^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1255^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mLocally unbound variable.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1256^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1257^I[37m;; module-symbol-binding module symbol opt-value[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1258^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1259^I[37m;; return the binding of a variable specified by name within[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1260^I[37m;; a given module, signalling an error if the variable is unbound.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1261^I[37m;; If the OPT-VALUE is passed, then instead of signalling an error,[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1262^I[37m;; return OPT-VALUE.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1263^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1264^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-symbol-binding[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1265^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1266^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1267^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([36mvariable-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvar[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1268^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnull?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1269^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mopt-val[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1270^I[37m^I    [39;49;00m([36merror[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[33mUnbound variable.[39;49;00m[33m"[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1271^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1272^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1273^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1274^I[37m;;; {Adding Variables to Modules}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1275^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1276^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1277^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1278^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1279^I[37m;; module-make-local-var! module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1280^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1281^I[37m;; ensure a variable for V in the local namespace of M.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1282^I[37m;; If no variable was already there, then create a new and uninitialzied[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1283^I[37m;; variable.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1284^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1285^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-make-local-var![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1286^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mor[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mb[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31mv[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1287^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mvariable?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mb[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1288^I[37m^I     [39;49;00m([34mbegin[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1290^I[37m^I       [39;49;00m[31mb[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1291^I[37m      [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-binder[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

  1299^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1300^I[37m;; module-ensure-local-variable! module symbol[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1301^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1322^I[37m[39;49;00m$

  1324^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1325^I[37m;; make sure that a symbol is undefined in the local namespace of M.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1334^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1335^I[37m;; MODULE-FOR-EACH -- exported[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1336^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1338^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1340^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mobarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-obarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1341^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mdo[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mindex[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m0[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m+[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mindex[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m1[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1342^I[37m^I [39;49;00m([32mend[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mvector-length[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mobarray[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$

  1346^I[37m^I [39;49;00m([32mproc[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbucket[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mbucket[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$

  1348^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1349^I[37m[39;49;00m$

  1353^I[37m[39;49;00m$

  1362^I[37m^I^I      [39;49;00m([36mvector-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mobarray[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mi[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$

  1364^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1365^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1366^I[37m;;; {Low Level Bootstrapping}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1367^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1368^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1369^I[37m;; make-root-module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1370^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1371^I[37m;; A root module uses the pre-modules-obarray as its obarray.  This[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1372^I[37m;; special obarray accumulates all bindings that have been established[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1373^I[37m;; before the module system is fully booted.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1374^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1375^I[37m;; (The obarray continues to be used by code that has been closed over[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1376^I[37m;;  before the module system has been booted.)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1377^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1378^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mmake-root-module[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1379^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m0[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1380^I[37m    [39;49;00m([36mset-module-obarray![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m%get-pre-modules-obarray[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1381^I[37m    [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1382^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1383^I[37m;; make-scm-module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1384^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1385^I[37m;; The root interface is a module that uses the same obarray as the[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1386^I[37m;; root module.  It does not allow new definitions, tho.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1387^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1388^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mmake-scm-module[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1389^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmake-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m0[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1390^I[37m    [39;49;00m([36mset-module-obarray![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36m%get-pre-modules-obarray[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1391^I[37m    [39;49;00m([32mset-module-eval-closure![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mstandard-interface-eval-closure[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1392^I[37m    [39;49;00m[31mm[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1393^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1394^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1395^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1396^I[37m;;; {Module-based Loading}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1397^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1398^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1399^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36msave-module-excursion[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mthunk[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1400^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32minner-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcurrent-module[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1401^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([32mouter-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1402^I[37m    [39;49;00m([36mdynamic-wind[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m()[37m[39;49;00m$
  1403^I[37m^I^I    [39;49;00m([34mset![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mouter-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcurrent-module[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1404^I[37m^I^I    [39;49;00m([36mset-current-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minner-module[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1405^I[37m^I^I    [39;49;00m([34mset![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minner-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1406^I[37m^I^I  [39;49;00m[31mthunk[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1407^I[37m^I^I  [39;49;00m([34mlambda[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m()[37m[39;49;00m$
  1408^I[37m^I^I    [39;49;00m([34mset![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minner-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcurrent-module[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1409^I[37m^I^I    [39;49;00m([36mset-current-module[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mouter-module[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

  1411^I[37m[39;49;00m$

  1413^I[37m[39;49;00m$

  1415^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36msave-module-excursion[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1424^I[37m^I^I       [39;49;00m[31mfilename[39;49;00m))))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1425^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1426^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1427^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1428^I[37m;;; {MODULE-REF -- exported}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1429^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1430^I[37m;; Returns the value of a variable called NAME in MODULE or any of its[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1431^I[37m;; used modules.  If there is no such variable, then if the optional third[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1434^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mrest[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

  1449^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$

  1457^I[37m;; variable, it is added first.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$

  1460^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-local-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1461^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mif[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1462^I[37m^I[39;49;00m([34mbegin[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1463^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m([36mvariable-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvalue[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$

  1466^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m([32mvariable-set-name-hint![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1467^I[37m^I  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-add![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m)))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1468^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1469^I[37m;; MODULE-DEFINED? -- exported[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1470^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1471^I[37m;; Return #t iff NAME is defined in MODULE (or in a module that MODULE[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1472^I[37m;; uses)[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1473^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1474^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-defined?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1475^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-variable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mname[39;49;00m)))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1476^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mand[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mvariable-bound?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mvariable[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1477^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1478^I[37m;; MODULE-USE! module interface[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1479^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1480^I[37m;; Add INTERFACE to the list of interfaces used by MODULE.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1481^I[37m;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1482^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-use![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minterface[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1483^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mset-module-uses![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1484^I[37m^I^I    [39;49;00m([36mcons[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minterface[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mdelq![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31minterface[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-uses[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1485^I[37m  [39;49;00m([36mmodule-modified[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mmodule[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1486^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1487^I[37m[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1488^I[37m;;; {Recursive Namespaces}[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1489^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1490^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1491^I[37m;;; A hierarchical namespace emerges if we consider some module to be[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1492^I[37m;;; root, and variables bound to modules as nested namespaces.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1493^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1494^I[37m;;; The routines in this file manage variable names in hierarchical namespace.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1495^I[37m;;; Each variable name is a list of elements, looked up in successively nested[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1496^I[37m;;; modules.[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1497^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1498^I[37m;;;^I^I(nested-ref some-root-module '(foo bar baz))[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1499^I[37m;;;^I^I=> <value of a variable named baz in the module bound to bar in[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1500^I[37m;;;^I^I    the module bound to foo in some-root-module>[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1501^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1502^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1503^I[37m;;; There are:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1504^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1505^I[37m;;;^I;; a-root is a module[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1506^I[37m;;;^I;; name is a list of symbols[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1507^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1508^I[37m;;;^Inested-ref a-root name[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1509^I[37m;;;^Inested-set! a-root name val[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1510^I[37m;;;^Inested-define! a-root name val[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1511^I[37m;;;^Inested-remove! a-root name[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1512^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1513^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1514^I[37m;;; (current-module) is a natural choice for a-root so for convenience there are[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1515^I[37m;;; also:[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1516^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1517^I[37m;;;^Ilocal-ref name^I^I==^Inested-ref (current-module) name[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1518^I[37m;;;^Ilocal-set! name val^I==^Inested-set! (current-module) name val[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1519^I[37m;;;^Ilocal-define! name val^I==^Inested-define! (current-module) name val[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1520^I[37m;;;^Ilocal-remove! name^I==^Inested-remove! (current-module) name[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1521^I[37m;;;[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1522^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1523^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1524^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnested-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1525^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1526^I[37m^I     [39;49;00m([32melts[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1527^I[37m    [39;49;00m([34mcond[39;49;00m[37m[39;49;00m$
  1528^I[37m     [39;49;00m(([36mnull?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m)[37m^I^I[39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1529^I[37m     [39;49;00m(([36mnot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule?[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m))[37m^I[39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1530^I[37m     [39;49;00m([34melse[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([32mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mmodule-ref[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mcar[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[31m#f[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m([36mcdr[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31melts[39;49;00m))))))[37m[39;49;00m$
  1531^I[37m[39;49;00m$
  1532^I([34mdefine[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([36mnested-set![39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mnames[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mval[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
  1533^I[37m  [39;49;00m([34mlet[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mloop[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m(([32mcur[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mroot[39;49;00m)[37m[39;49;00m$
